Implement the following plan:

# P1 收尾 + P0 测试覆盖 — 实施计划

## Context

TODO.md P1 剩余两项：CI 流水线 + 集成测试。
P0 heartbeat 代码已完成（heartbeat.py, memorytree_daemon.py, _config_utils.py, _lock_utils.py, _alert_utils.py, _log_utils.py），但零测试覆盖。需要补充 P0 模块的单元测试 + heartbeat 集成测试，才能达到 80% 覆盖率并关闭 P0 测试子项。

## 执行顺序（4 个 commit）

### Commit 1: CI 流水线

新建 .github/workflows/ci.yml

- 触发：push master + PR to master
- 矩阵：Python 3.11/3.12/3.13 × ubuntu/macos/windows（9 组合）
- 步骤：checkout → setup-python → pip install coverage → coverage run -m unittest discover -s tests → coverage report --fail-under=80
- ubuntu+3.13 上传 coverage.xml artifact
- 零外部依赖（coverage 是唯一 CI 依赖）

### Commit 2: P0 模块单元测试

新建 tests/test_heartbeat_modules.py — 统一测试 P0 四个模块

测试 _config_utils.py：
- load_config() 无文件时返回默认值
- load_config() 解析合法 TOML
- interval_to_seconds() 各种格式（"5m"→300, "300s"→300, "1h"→3600）
- save_config() + load_config() round-trip
- register_project() 添加 + 去重

测试 _lock_utils.py：
- acquire_lock() 首次成功
- acquire_lock() 已锁定时失败
- release_lock() 后可重新获取
- 过期锁自动回收（写入不存在的 PID）
- 损坏锁文件视为过期

测试 _alert_utils.py：
- write_alert() 创建文件 + 去重 + count 递增
- read_alerts() 文件不存在返回空列表
- write_alert_with_threshold() 达到阈值才写
- reset_failure_count() 清除计数

测试 _log_utils.py：
- setup_logging() 返回配置好的 logger
- setup_logging() 幂等（不重复 handler）

所有测试用 tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() + unittest.mock.patch 隔离文件系统。

### Commit 3: 集成测试

新建 tests/test_integration.py

场景 1：init → upgrade → import 端到端
- 临时目录 → 调用 create_memory_dirs() + scaffold_content_files() → 验证目录结构
- 调用 upgrade-memorytree.py 的 detect_state() → 验证状态为 installed
- 创建 mock Claude transcript → parse_claude_transcript() → import_transcript() → 验证 raw/clean/manifest 文件

场景 2：discover 批量扫描
- 临时目录模拟三个客户端 transcript 布局
- unittest.mock.patch 替换 default_client_roots() 指向临时目录
- 调用 discover_source_files() → 验证全部发现

场景 3：heartbeat 敏感信息扫描
- 导入 heartbeat.py 的 SENSITIVE_PATTERNS + _scan_sensitive()
- 测试各种模式（API key, password, Bearer token）命中/不命中

场景 4：heartbeat 集成
- git init 临时 repo → 创建 Memory/ 结构 → 放入 mock transcript
- patch config/client_roots → 调用 heartbeat 主逻辑
- 验证 transcript 已导入 + git commit 已生成

### Commit 4: 更新 TODO.md

标记 P1 CI 流水线、集成测试、P0 测试为已完成。

1→"""PID-based lock file for heartbeat single-instance enforcement."""
     2→
     3→from __future__ import annotations
     4→
     5→import logging
     6→import os
     7→import sys
     8→from pathlib import Path
     9→
    10→log = logging.getLogger("memorytree")
    11→
    12→
    13→def lock_path() -> Path:
    14→    return Path.home() / ".memorytree" / "heartbeat.lock"
    15→
    16→
    17→def acquire_lock() -> bool:
    18→    """Try to acquire the heartbeat lock. Returns True on success."""
    19→    path = lock_path()
    20→    path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    21→
    22→    if path.exists():
    23→        try:
    24→            stored_pid = int(path.read_text(encoding="utf-8").strip())
    25→        except (OSError, ValueError):
    26→            # Corrupt lock file — treat as stale
    27→            log.warning("Corrupt lock file detected, removing: %s", path)
    28→            _remove_lock(path)
    29→        else:
    30→            if _is_process_alive(stored_pid):
    31→                return False
    32→            # Stale lock from a dead process
    33→            log.warning("Stale lock detected (PID %d is dead), reclaiming.", stored_pid)
    34→            _remove_lock(path)
    35→
    36→    # Use exclusive create to prevent TOCTOU race
    37→    try:
    38→        fd = os.open(str(path), os.O_CREAT | os.O_EXCL | os.O_WRONLY)
    39→        os.write(fd, str(os.getpid()).encode("utf-8"))
    40→        os.close(fd)
    41→    except FileExistsError:
    42→        # Another process created the lock between our check and create
    43→        return False
    44→    except OSError:
    45→        return False
    46→    return True
    47→
    48→
    49→def release_lock() -> None:
    50→    """Release the heartbeat lock."""
    51→    _remove_lock(lock_path())
    52→
    53→
    54→def read_lock_pid() -> int | None:
    55→    """Read the PID from the lock file, or None if not locked."""
    56→    path = lock_path()
    57→    if not path.exists():
    58→        return None
    59→    try:
    60→        return int(path.read_text(encoding="utf-8").strip())
    61→    except (OSError, ValueError):
    62→        return None
    63→
    64→
    65→def _is_process_alive(pid: int) -> bool:
    66→    """Check whether a process with the given PID is still running."""
    67→    if pid <= 0:
    68→        return False
    69→    if sys.platform == "win32":
    70→        return _is_process_alive_windows(pid)
    71→    return _is_process_alive_unix(pid)
    72→
    73→
    74→def _is_process_alive_unix(pid: int) -> bool:
    75→    try:
    76→        os.kill(pid, 0)
    77→        return True
    78→    except ProcessLookupError:
    79→        return False
    80→    except PermissionError:
    81→        # Process exists but we can't signal it
    82→        return True
    83→
    84→
    85→def _is_process_alive_windows(pid: int) -> bool:
    86→    try:
    87→        import ctypes
    88→        kernel32 = ctypes.windll.kernel32  # type: ignore[attr-defined]
    89→        PROCESS_QUERY_LIMITED_INFORMATION = 0x1000
    90→        handle = kernel32.OpenProcess(PROCESS_QUERY_LIMITED_INFORMATION, False, pid)
    91→        if handle:
    92→            kernel32.CloseHandle(handle)
    93→            return True
    94→        return False
    95→    except Exception:
    96→        return False
    97→
    98→
    99→def _remove_lock(path: Path) -> None:
   100→    try:
   101→        path.unlink(missing_ok=True)
   102→    except OSError:
   103→        pass
   104→

1→"""Logging setup for heartbeat — file rotation + stderr output."""
     2→
     3→from __future__ import annotations
     4→
     5→import logging
     6→import sys
     7→from datetime import datetime, timezone
     8→from pathlib import Path
     9→
    10→LOGGER_NAME = "memorytree"
    11→
    12→
    13→def setup_logging(log_level: str = "info") -> logging.Logger:
    14→    """Configure the memorytree logger with file and stderr handlers."""
    15→    logger = logging.getLogger(LOGGER_NAME)
    16→    if logger.handlers:
    17→        return logger
    18→
    19→    level = _resolve_level(log_level)
    20→    logger.setLevel(level)
    21→    formatter = logging.Formatter(
    22→        "%(asctime)s [%(levelname)s] %(message)s",
    23→        datefmt="%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%S",
    24→    )
    25→
    26→    # Stderr handler
    27→    stderr_handler = logging.StreamHandler(sys.stderr)
    28→    stderr_handler.setLevel(level)
    29→    stderr_handler.setFormatter(formatter)
    30→    logger.addHandler(stderr_handler)
    31→
    32→    # File handler (date-based rotation)
    33→    log_file = _log_file_path()
    34→    log_file.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    35→    try:
    36→        file_handler = logging.FileHandler(log_file, encoding="utf-8")
    37→        file_handler.setLevel(level)
    38→        file_handler.setFormatter(formatter)
    39→        logger.addHandler(file_handler)
    40→    except OSError:
    41→        logger.warning("Could not open log file: %s", log_file)
    42→
    43→    return logger
    44→
    45→
    46→def get_logger() -> logging.Logger:
    47→    """Get the memorytree logger (must call setup_logging first)."""
    48→    return logging.getLogger(LOGGER_NAME)

    51→def _log_file_path() -> Path:

    56→def _resolve_level(level_str: str) -> int:

    59→        "info": logging.INFO,
    60→        "warn": logging.WARNING,
    61→        "warning": logging.WARNING,

    22→def read_alerts() -> list[dict]:
    23→    """Read all pending alerts. Returns empty list if file missing or malformed."""
    24→    path = alerts_path()
    25→    if not path.exists():
    26→        return []
    27→    try:
    28→        data = json.loads(path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    29→    except (OSError, json.JSONDecodeError):
    30→        return []
    31→    if not isinstance(data, list):
    32→        return []

    35→
    36→def write_alert(
    37→    project: str,
    38→    alert_type: str,
    39→    message: str,
    40→) -> None:
    41→    """Append or dedup an alert. Dedup key is (project, type)."""
    42→    alerts = read_alerts()
    43→    now = datetime.now(timezone.utc).replace(microsecond=0).isoformat().replace("+00:00", "Z")
    44→
    45→    # Dedup: find existing alert with same project+type, build new list
    46→    found = False
    47→    new_alerts = []
    48→    for alert in alerts:
    49→        if alert.get("project") == project and alert.get("type") == alert_type:
    50→            new_alerts.append(
    51→                {
    52→                    **alert,
    53→                    "timestamp": now,
    54→                    "message": message,
    55→                    "count": alert.get("count", 1) + 1,
    56→                }
    57→            )
    58→            found = True
    59→        else:
    60→            new_alerts.append(alert)
    61→
    62→    if not found:
    63→        new_alerts.append(
    64→            {
    65→                "timestamp": now,
    66→                "project": project,
    67→                "type": alert_type,
    68→                "message": message,
    69→                "count": 1,
    70→            }
    71→        )
    72→
    73→    # Cap at MAX_ALERTS, drop oldest first
    74→    if len(new_alerts) > MAX_ALERTS:
    75→        new_alerts = new_alerts[-MAX_ALERTS:]
    76→
    77→    _save_alerts(new_alerts)
    78→
    79→
    80→def write_alert_with_threshold(
    81→    project: str,
    82→    alert_type: str,
    83→    message: str,
    84→) -> None:
    85→    """Write an alert only after FAILURE_THRESHOLD consecutive failures for the same project+type."""
    86→    counts = _read_failure_counts()
    87→    key = f"{project}::{alert_type}"
    88→    current = counts.get(key, 0) + 1
    89→    new_counts = {**counts, key: current}
    90→    _save_failure_counts(new_counts)
    91→
    92→    if current >= FAILURE_THRESHOLD:
    93→        write_alert(project, alert_type, message)
    94→
    95→
    96→def reset_failure_count(project: str, alert_type: str) -> None:
    97→    """Reset the consecutive failure counter on success."""
    98→    counts = _read_failure_counts()
    99→    key = f"{project}::{alert_type}"
   100→    if key in counts:
   101→        new_counts = {k: v for k, v in counts.items() if k != key}
   102→        _save_failure_counts(new_counts)
   103→
   104→
   105→def clear_alerts() -> None:
   106→    """Remove all alerts (called after displaying to user)."""
   107→    path = alerts_path()
   108→    if path.exists():
   109→        try:
   110→            path.unlink()
   111→        except OSError:
   112→            pass
   113→
   114→
   115→def format_alerts_for_display(alerts: list[dict]) -> str:
   116→    """Format alerts as a human-readable text block."""
   117→    if not alerts:
   118→        return ""
   119→    lines = []
   120→    for alert in alerts:
   121→        count_suffix = f" (x{alert['count']})" if alert.get("count", 1) > 1 else ""
   122→        lines.append(
   123→            f"  [{alert.get('type', 'unknown')}] {alert.get('project', '?')}: "
   124→            f"{alert.get('message', '')}{count_suffix}"
   125→        )
   126→    return "\n".join(lines)
   127→
   128→
   129→def _save_alerts(alerts: list[dict]) -> None:
   130→    path = alerts_path()
   131→    path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
   132→    path.write_text(
   133→        json.dumps(alerts, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2) + "\n",
   134→        encoding="utf-8",
   135→    )
   136→
   137→
   138→def _read_failure_counts() -> dict[str, int]:
   139→    path = _failure_state_path()
   140→    if not path.exists():
   141→        return {}
   142→    try:
   143→        data = json.loads(path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
   144→    except (OSError, json.JSONDecodeError):
   145→        return {}
   146→    if not isinstance(data, dict):
   147→        return {}
   148→    return data
   149→
   150→
   151→def _save_failure_counts(counts: dict[str, int]) -> None:
   152→    path = _failure_state_path()

    39→def main() -> int:
    40→    config = load_config()
    41→    logger = setup_logging(config.log_level)
    42→
    43→    if not acquire_lock():
    44→        logger.info("Another heartbeat instance is running. Exiting.")
    45→        write_alert("global", "lock_held", "Heartbeat exited: another instance held the lock.")
    46→        return 0
    47→
    48→    try:
    49→        return _run_heartbeat(config)
    50→    finally:
    51→        release_lock()
    52→
    53→
    54→def _run_heartbeat(config: Config) -> int:
    55→    logger = get_logger()
    56→
    57→    if not config.projects:
    58→        logger.info("No projects registered in config.toml. Nothing to do.")
    59→        return 0
    60→
    61→    logger.info("Heartbeat started. %d project(s) registered.", len(config.projects))
    62→
    63→    for entry in config.projects:
    64→        project_path = entry.resolved_path()
    65→        if not project_path.exists():
    66→            logger.warning("Project path does not exist, skipping: %s", project_path)
    67→            continue
    68→        try:
    69→            _process_project(config, project_path, entry.name or project_path.name)
    70→        except Exception:
    71→            logger.exception("Error processing project: %s", project_path)
    72→            write_alert_with_threshold(
    73→                project=project_path.as_posix(),
    74→                alert_type="push_failed",
    75→                message=f"Heartbeat error for project: {project_path.name}",
    76→            )
    77→
    78→    logger.info("Heartbeat finished.")
    79→    return 0
    80→
    81→
    82→def _process_project(config: Config, project_path: Path, project_name: str) -> None:
    83→    logger = get_logger()
    84→    repo_slug = slugify(project_name, fallback="project")
    85→    global_root = Path.home() / ".memorytree" / "transcripts"
    86→
    87→    # Discover and import new transcripts
    88→    discovered = discover_source_files()
    89→    imported_count = 0
    90→
    91→    for client, source in discovered:
    92→        try:
    93→            parsed = parse_transcript(client, source)
    94→        except Exception:
    95→            logger.debug("Failed to parse %s, skipping.", source)
    96→            continue
    97→
    98→        if not transcript_has_content(parsed):
    99→            continue
   100→
   101→        if not transcript_matches_repo(parsed, project_path, repo_slug):
   102→            continue
   103→
   104→        # Sensitive info scan on cleaned content
   105→        _scan_sensitive(parsed, project_path)
   106→
   107→        try:
   108→            import_transcript(
   109→                parsed=parsed,
   110→                root=project_path,
   111→                global_root=global_root,
   112→                project_slug=repo_slug,
   113→                raw_upload_permission="not-set",
   114→                mirror_to_repo=True,
   115→            )
   116→            imported_count += 1
   117→        except Exception:
   118→            logger.exception("Failed to import transcript: %s", source)
   119→
   120→    if imported_count == 0:
   121→        logger.info("[%s] No new transcripts to import.", project_name)
   122→        return
   123→
   124→    logger.info("[%s] Imported %d transcript(s).", project_name, imported_count)
   125→
   126→    # Git commit + push
   127→    _git_commit_and_push(config, project_path, project_name, imported_count)
   128→
   129→
   130→def _scan_sensitive(parsed: ParsedTranscript, project_path: Path) -> None:
   131→    """Scan transcript messages for sensitive patterns. Warn only, never delete."""
   132→    logger = get_logger()
   133→    for msg in parsed.messages:
   134→        for pattern in SENSITIVE_PATTERNS:
   135→            if pattern.search(msg.text):
   136→                logger.warning(
   137→                    "Sensitive pattern detected in transcript %s (project: %s, role: %s)",
   138→                    parsed.source_path,
   139→                    project_path.name,
   140→                    msg.role,
   141→                )
   142→                write_alert(
   143→                    project=project_path.as_posix(),
   144→                    alert_type="sensitive_match",
   145→                    message=f"Sensitive pattern in transcript: {parsed.source_path.name}",
   146→                )
   147→                return  # One alert per transcript is enough
   148→
   149→
   150→def _git_commit_and_push(config: Config, project_path: Path, project_name: str, count: int) -> None:
   151→    logger = get_logger()
   152→
   153→    # Check for changes in Memory/
   154→    status = _git(project_path, "status", "--porcelain", "Memory/")
   155→    if not status.strip():
   156→        logger.info("[%s] No git changes in Memory/.", project_name)
   157→        return
   158→
   159→    # Stage and commit
   160→    _git(project_path, "add", "Memory/")
   161→    _git(
   162→        project_path,
   163→        "commit",
   164→        "-m",
   165→        f"memorytree(transcripts): import {count} transcript(s)",
   166→    )
   167→    logger.info("[%s] Committed %d transcript import(s).", project_name, count)
   168→
   169→    if not config.auto_push:
   170→        logger.info("[%s] auto_push disabled, skipping push.", project_name)
   171→        return
   172→
   173→    # Remote pre-check
   174→    remotes = _git(project_path, "remote")
   175→    if not remotes.strip():
   176→        logger.warning("[%s] No git remote configured, skipping push.", project_name)
   177→        write_alert(
   178→            project=project_path.as_posix(),
   179→            alert_type="no_remote",
   180→            message="Push skipped: no Git remote configured.",
   181→        )
   182→        return
   183→
   184→    # Push with one retry
   185→    if not _try_push(project_path, project_name):
   186→        logger.warning("[%s] Push failed, retrying once...", project_name)
   187→        if not _try_push(project_path, project_name):
   188→            logger.error("[%s] Push failed after retry.", project_name)
   189→            write_alert_with_threshold(
   190→                project=project_path.as_posix(),
   191→                alert_type="push_failed",
   192→                message="Push failed after retry.",
   193→            )
   194→            return
   195→
   196→    reset_failure_count(project_path.as_posix(), "push_failed")
   197→
   198→
   199→def _try_push(project_path: Path, project_name: str) -> bool:
   200→    try:
   201→        _git(project_path, "push")
   202→        get_logger().info("[%s] Pushed successfully.", project_name)
   203→        return True
   204→    except subprocess.CalledProcessError:
   205→        return False
   206→
   207→
   208→def _git(cwd: Path, *args: str) -> str:
   209→    result = subprocess.run(
   210→        ["git", *args],
   211→        cwd=cwd,
   212→        capture_output=True,
   213→        text=True,
   214→        timeout=120,
   215→    )
   216→    if result.returncode != 0 and args[0] not in ("status", "remote"):
   217→        raise subprocess.CalledProcessError(
   218→            result.returncode, ["git", *args], result.stdout, result.stderr
   219→        )
   220→    return result.stdout
   221→
   222→
   223→if __name__ == "__main__":
   224→    sys.exit(main())
   225→

1→# memorytree-workflow Skill 开发待办
     2→
     3→## 背景
     4→
     5→本仓库是 MemoryTree 记忆系统的 Skill 实现，从 `beyondchenlin/memorytree` 独立拆出。
     6→消费端项目（普通项目）通过安装此 Skill 获得记忆管理能力。
     7→
     8→## 当前核心问题
     9→
    10→大模型不可靠 — 会忘记执行 chat_log 记录、transcript 导入等机械性流程。
    11→需要把这些确定性工作交给后台进程，大模型只做轻量的摘要和状态更新。
    12→
    13→## 架构决策
    14→
    15→### 定时心跳（单次执行 + OS 调度，零 token 消耗）
    16→- 全局单实例: 1 台电脑 = 1 个定时任务，扫描所有项目
    17→- 定时扫描客户端 transcript 目录（~/.claude/projects/、~/.codex/sessions/、~/.gemini/）
    18→- 每次执行: 扫描 → 增量导入 → 清洗 → git commit + push → 退出
    19→- 心跳间隔可配置（默认 5 分钟）
    20→- 运行方式: OS 原生定时任务（cron / launchd / Task Scheduler），tmux 仅用于开发调试
    21→- Git 策略: **默认 auto_push = true**（记忆数据安全优先，防止本地丢失）
    22→
    23→### 大模型（对话时才介入，省 token）
    24→- 只写当轮 chat_log 摘要（几行文字）
    25→- 只更新 goal/todo 状态
    26→- 不负责 transcript 导入、清洗、提交
    27→

    50→  - **默认 auto_push = true**（记忆是用户资产，本地丢失不可恢复）
    51→  - 首次安装时提示用户确认 push 行为，之后静默执行

    75→

    42→def config_path() -> Path:

    45→
    46→def load_config() -> Config:
    47→    """Load config.toml, falling back to defaults on any error."""
    48→    path = config_path()
    49→    if not path.exists():
    50→        log.info("config.toml not found, using defaults.")
    51→        return Config()
    52→    try:
    53→        with path.open("rb") as fh:
    54→            raw = tomllib.load(fh)
    55→    except (OSError, tomllib.TOMLDecodeError) as exc:
    56→        log.error("Failed to parse config.toml: %s. Using defaults.", exc)
    57→        return Config()
    58→    return _parse_raw(raw)
    59→
    60→
    61→def _parse_raw(raw: dict) -> Config:
    62→    interval = raw.get("heartbeat_interval", DEFAULT_HEARTBEAT_INTERVAL)
    63→    if not isinstance(interval, str) or not _is_valid_interval(interval):
    64→        log.warning("Invalid heartbeat_interval '%s', using default '%s'.", interval, DEFAULT_HEARTBEAT_INTERVAL)
    65→        interval = DEFAULT_HEARTBEAT_INTERVAL
    66→
    67→    auto_push = raw.get("auto_push", DEFAULT_AUTO_PUSH)
    68→    if not isinstance(auto_push, bool):
    69→        log.warning("Invalid auto_push value '%s', using default %s.", auto_push, DEFAULT_AUTO_PUSH)
    70→        auto_push = DEFAULT_AUTO_PUSH
    71→
    72→    log_level = raw.get("log_level", DEFAULT_LOG_LEVEL)
    73→    if not isinstance(log_level, str) or log_level.lower() not in VALID_LOG_LEVELS:
    74→        log.warning("Invalid log_level '%s', using default '%s'.", log_level, DEFAULT_LOG_LEVEL)
    75→        log_level = DEFAULT_LOG_LEVEL
    76→    log_level = log_level.lower()
    77→
    78→    watch_dirs: list[str] = []
    79→    raw_dirs = raw.get("watch_dirs", [])
    80→    if isinstance(raw_dirs, list):
    81→        for d in raw_dirs:
    82→            if isinstance(d, str):
    83→                watch_dirs.append(d)
    84→
    85→    projects: list[ProjectEntry] = []
    86→    raw_projects = raw.get("projects", [])
    87→    if isinstance(raw_projects, list):
    88→        for entry in raw_projects:
    89→            if isinstance(entry, dict) and isinstance(entry.get("path"), str):
    90→                projects.append(
    91→                    ProjectEntry(
    92→                        path=entry["path"],
    93→                        name=str(entry.get("name", "")),
    94→                    )
    95→                )
    96→
    97→    return Config(
    98→        heartbeat_interval=interval,
    99→        watch_dirs=watch_dirs,
   100→        projects=projects,
   101→        auto_push=auto_push,
   102→        log_level=log_level,

   104→
   105→
   106→def interval_to_seconds(interval: str) -> int:
   107→    """Convert an interval string like '5m' or '300s' to seconds."""
   108→    match = re.fullmatch(r"(\d+)\s*(s|m|h)", interval.strip().lower())
   109→    if not match:
   110→        return interval_to_seconds(DEFAULT_HEARTBEAT_INTERVAL)
   111→    value = int(match.group(1))
   112→    unit = match.group(2)
   113→    if value <= 0:
   114→        return interval_to_seconds(DEFAULT_HEARTBEAT_INTERVAL)
   115→    multiplier = {"s": 1, "m": 60, "h": 3600}
   116→    return value * multiplier[unit]
   117→
   118→
   119→def save_config(cfg: Config) -> None:
   120→    """Write config back to config.toml."""
   121→    path = config_path()
   122→    path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
   123→    lines = [
   124→        f'heartbeat_interval = "{cfg.heartbeat_interval}"',
   125→        f"auto_push = {'true' if cfg.auto_push else 'false'}",
   126→        f'log_level = "{cfg.log_level}"',
   127→    ]
   128→    if cfg.watch_dirs:
   129→        items = ", ".join(f'"{d}"' for d in cfg.watch_dirs)
   130→        lines.append(f"watch_dirs = [{items}]")
   131→    else:
   132→        lines.append("watch_dirs = []")
   133→
   134→    lines.append("")
   135→    for project in cfg.projects:
   136→        lines.append("[[projects]]")
   137→        lines.append(f'path = "{project.path}"')
   138→        if project.name:
   139→            lines.append(f'name = "{project.name}"')
   140→        lines.append("")
   141→
   142→    path.write_text("\n".join(lines) + "\n", encoding="utf-8")
   143→
   144→
   145→def register_project(cfg: Config, repo_path: Path) -> Config:
   146→    """Add a project to the config if not already registered. Returns new Config."""
   147→    resolved = repo_path.resolve().as_posix()
   148→    for entry in cfg.projects:
   149→        if entry.resolved_path().as_posix() == resolved:
   150→            return cfg
   151→    new_projects = [*cfg.projects, ProjectEntry(path=resolved, name=repo_path.name)]
   152→    return Config(
   153→        heartbeat_interval=cfg.heartbeat_interval,
   154→        watch_dirs=list(cfg.watch_dirs),
   155→        projects=new_projects,
   156→        auto_push=cfg.auto_push,
   157→        log_level=cfg.log_level,
   158→    )

   161→def _is_valid_interval(value: str) -> bool:
   162→    match = re.fullmatch(r"(\d+)\s*(s|m|h)", value.strip().lower())
   163→    if not match:
   164→        return False
   165→    return int(match.group(1)) > 0

    17→    home = Path.home()
    18→    return {

    25→def discover_source_files(clients: set[str] | None = None) -> list[tuple[str, Path]]:
    26→    requested = clients or CLIENTS
    27→    roots = default_client_roots()
    28→    patterns = {
    29→        "codex": ["sessions/**/*.jsonl"],
    30→        "claude": ["projects/**/*.jsonl"],
    31→        "gemini": [
    32→            "tmp/*/checkpoints/**/*.json",
    33→            "tmp/*/checkpoints/**/*.jsonl",
    34→            "history/**/*.json",
    35→            "history/**/*.jsonl",
    36→            "chats/**/*.json",
    37→            "chats/**/*.jsonl",
    38→        ],
    39→    }
    40→    matches: list[tuple[str, Path]] = []
    41→    seen: set[str] = set()
    42→    for client in sorted(requested):
    43→        root = roots.get(client)
    44→        if root is None or not root.exists():
    45→            continue
    46→        for pattern in patterns[client]:
    47→            for path in root.glob(pattern):
    48→                if not path.is_file():
    49→                    continue
    50→                key = path.resolve().as_posix().lower()
    51→                if key in seen:
    52→                    continue
    53→                seen.add(key)
    54→                matches.append((client, path.resolve()))
    55→    matches.sort(
    56→        key=lambda item: (safe_file_mtime(item[1]), item[1].as_posix().lower()),
    57→        reverse=True,
    58→    )
    59→    return matches
    60→
    61→
    62→def infer_project_slug(parsed: ParsedTranscript) -> str:
    63→    if parsed.cwd:
    64→        try:
    65→            cwd_path = Path(parsed.cwd)
    66→            return slugify(cwd_path.name, fallback="project")
    67→        except OSError:
    68→            pass
    69→    if parsed.client == "claude":
    70→        parent_name = parsed.source_path.parent.name
    71→        parent_name = re.sub(r"^[a-z]--", "", parent_name.lower())
    72→        return slugify(parent_name, fallback="project")
    73→    if parsed.client == "gemini" and parsed.source_path.parent.name:
    74→        return slugify(parsed.source_path.parent.name, fallback="project")
    75→    return "unknown-project"

   108→def transcript_has_content(parsed: ParsedTranscript) -> bool:
   109→    return bool(parsed.messages or parsed.tool_events)

   111→
   112→def write_clean_markdown(parsed: ParsedTranscript, manifest: dict[str, Any], path: Path) -> None:
   113→    lines = [
   114→        "---",
   115→        f"client: {manifest['client']}",
   116→        f"project: {manifest['project']}",
   117→        f"session_id: {manifest['session_id']}",
   118→        f"title: {yaml_escape(manifest['title'])}",
   119→        f"started_at: {manifest['started_at']}",
   120→        f"imported_at: {manifest['imported_at']}",
   121→        f"cwd: {yaml_escape(manifest['cwd'])}",
   122→        f"branch: {yaml_escape(manifest['branch'])}",
   123→        f"raw_source_path: {yaml_escape(manifest['raw_source_path'])}",
   124→        f"raw_sha256: {manifest['raw_sha256']}",
   125→        f"raw_upload_permission: {manifest['raw_upload_permission']}",
   126→        f"cleaning_mode: {manifest['cleaning_mode']}",
   127→        "---",
   128→        "",
   129→        f"# {manifest['title'] or manifest['session_id']}",
   130→        "",
   131→        "## Metadata",
   132→        f"- Client: `{manifest['client']}`",
   133→        f"- Project: `{manifest['project']}`",
   134→        f"- Session ID: `{manifest['session_id']}`",
   135→        f"- Started At: `{manifest['started_at']}`",
   136→        f"- Imported At: `{manifest['imported_at']}`",
   137→        f"- Raw SHA256: `{manifest['raw_sha256']}`",
   138→        f"- Raw Source: `{manifest['raw_source_path']}`",
   139→        f"- Repo Raw Path: `{manifest['repo_raw_path']}`",
   140→        f"- Repo Clean Path: `{manifest['repo_clean_path']}`",
   141→        "",
   142→        "## Messages",
   143→    ]
   144→
   145→    if parsed.messages:
   146→        for index, message in enumerate(parsed.messages, start=1):
   147→            lines.extend(
   148→                [
   149→                    f"### {index}. {message.role}",
   150→                    f"- Timestamp: `{message.timestamp or manifest['started_at']}`",
   151→                    "",
   152→                    message.text,
   153→                    "",
   154→                ]
   155→            )
   156→    else:
   157→        lines.extend(
   158→            [
   159→                "No user or assistant messages were extracted deterministically from the source transcript.",
   160→                "",
   161→            ]
   162→        )
   163→
   164→    lines.append("## Tool Events")
   165→    if parsed.tool_events:
   166→        for event in parsed.tool_events:
   167→            lines.append(f"- `{event.timestamp or manifest['started_at']}` {event.summary}")
   168→    else:
   169→        lines.append("- No tool events were extracted.")
   170→    lines.append("")
   171→
   172→    path.write_text("\n".join(lines), encoding="utf-8")
   173→
   174→
   175→def preserve_existing_import_timestamp(existing: dict[str, Any] | None, payload: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
   176→    if existing is None:
   177→        return payload
   178→    if manifest_signature(existing) != manifest_signature(payload):
   179→        return payload
   180→    preserved = dict(payload)
   181→    imported_at = existing.get("imported_at")
   182→    if isinstance(imported_at, str) and imported_at:
   183→        preserved["imported_at"] = imported_at
   184→    return preserved
   185→
   186→
   187→def manifest_signature(payload: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
   188→    return {key: value for key, value in payload.items() if key != "imported_at"}
   189→
   190→
   191→def manifest_changed(path: Path, payload: dict[str, Any]) -> bool:
   192→    if not path.exists():
   193→        return True
   194→    try:
   195→        current = json.loads(path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
   196→    except (OSError, json.JSONDecodeError):
   197→        return True
   198→    return current != payload
   199→
   200→
   201→def write_json(path: Path, payload: dict[str, Any]) -> None:
   202→    path.write_text(json.dumps(payload, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2) + "\n", encoding="utf-8")
   203→
   204→
   205→def append_jsonl(path: Path, payload: dict[str, Any]) -> None:
   206→    with path.open("a", encoding="utf-8") as handle:
   207→        handle.write(json.dumps(payload, ensure_ascii=False) + "\n")
   208→
   209→
   210→def copy_file(source: Path, destination: Path) -> None:
   211→    if source.resolve() == destination.resolve():
   212→        return
   213→    shutil.copy2(source, destination)
   214→

    63→def infer_client(client: str, source: Path) -> str:
    64→    if client != "auto":
    65→        return client
    66→    normalized = source.as_posix().lower()
    67→    if "/.codex/" in normalized or "rollout-" in source.name.lower():
    68→        return "codex"
    69→    if "/.claude/" in normalized or "/projects/" in normalized:
    70→        return "claude"
    71→    if "/.gemini/" in normalized or "checkpoint" in normalized:
    72→        return "gemini"
    73→    raise SystemExit(f"could not infer transcript client from source path: {source}")

   196→def parse_claude_transcript(path: Path) -> ParsedTranscript:
   197→    records = load_jsonl(path)
   198→    session_id = path.stem
   199→    title = path.stem
   200→    started_at = normalize_timestamp(path.stat().st_mtime)
   201→    cwd = ""
   202→    branch = ""
   203→    messages: list[TranscriptMessage] = []
   204→    tool_events: list[TranscriptToolEvent] = []
   205→
   206→    for record in records:
   207→        record_type = str(record.get("type") or "")
   208→        timestamp = normalize_timestamp(record.get("timestamp"), started_at)
   209→        session_id = str(record.get("sessionId") or session_id)
   210→        started_at = earliest_timestamp(started_at, record.get("timestamp"))
   211→        cwd = str(record.get("cwd") or cwd)
   212→        branch = str(record.get("gitBranch") or branch)
   213→
   214→        if record_type not in {"user", "assistant"}:
   215→            continue
   216→
   217→        message = ensure_dict(record.get("message"))
   218→        role = str(message.get("role") or record_type).lower()
   219→        text_parts: list[str] = []
   220→        content = message.get("content")
   221→        if isinstance(content, str):
   222→            text = content.strip()
   223→            if role in {"user", "assistant"} and text:
   224→                messages.append(TranscriptMessage(role=role, text=text, timestamp=timestamp))
   225→            continue
   226→
   227→        for block in ensure_list(content):
   228→            if isinstance(block, str):
   229→                if block.strip():
   230→                    text_parts.append(block.strip())
   231→                continue
   232→            if not isinstance(block, dict):
   233→                continue
   234→            block_type = str(block.get("type") or "").lower()
   235→            if block_type in TEXT_BLOCK_TYPES:
   236→                text = str(block.get("text") or "").strip()
   237→                if text:
   238→                    text_parts.append(text)
   239→                continue
   240→            if block_type in SKIP_BLOCK_TYPES:
   241→                continue
   242→            if block_type in TOOL_USE_TYPES:
   243→                name = str(block.get("name") or "tool_use")
   244→                tool_events.append(
   245→                    TranscriptToolEvent(
   246→                        summary=f"{name} input={summarize_value(block.get('input'))}",
   247→                        timestamp=timestamp,
   248→                    )
   249→                )
   250→                continue
   251→            if block_type in TOOL_RESULT_TYPES:
   252→                tool_use_id = str(block.get("tool_use_id") or "tool_result")
   253→                tool_events.append(
   254→                    TranscriptToolEvent(
   255→                        summary=f"{tool_use_id} output={summarize_value(block.get('content'))}",
   256→                        timestamp=timestamp,
   257→                    )
   258→                )
   259→
   260→        text = join_paragraphs(text_parts)
   261→        if role in {"user", "assistant"} and text:
   262→            messages.append(TranscriptMessage(role=role, text=text, timestamp=timestamp))
   263→
   264→    messages = deduplicate_messages(messages)
   265→    tool_events = deduplicate_tool_events(tool_events)
   266→
   267→    return ParsedTranscript(
   268→        client="claude",
   269→        session_id=session_id,
   270→        title=title,
   271→        started_at=started_at,
   272→        cwd=cwd,
   273→        branch=branch,
   274→        messages=messages,
   275→        tool_events=tool_events,
   276→        source_path=path,
   277→    )

   280→# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   281→# Gemini parser
   282→# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   283→
   284→
   285→def parse_gemini_transcript(path: Path) -> ParsedTranscript:
   286→    session_id = path.stem
   287→    title = path.stem
   288→    started_at = normalize_timestamp(path.stat().st_mtime)
   289→    cwd = ""
   290→    branch = ""
   291→    messages: list[TranscriptMessage] = []
   292→    tool_events: list[TranscriptToolEvent] = []
   293→
   294→    if path.suffix.lower() == ".jsonl":
   295→        payload: Any = load_jsonl(path)
   296→    else:
   297→        payload = json.loads(path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
   298→
   299→    first_meta = find_first_mapping_with_keys(payload, {"sessionId", "chatId", "cwd", "branch", "timestamp"})
   300→    if first_meta:
   301→        session_id = str(first_meta.get("sessionId") or first_meta.get("chatId") or first_meta.get("id") or session_id)
   302→        started_at = earliest_timestamp(started_at, first_meta.get("timestamp"))
   303→        cwd = str(first_meta.get("cwd") or first_meta.get("projectRoot") or cwd)
   304→        branch = str(first_meta.get("branch") or branch)
   305→
   306→    def visit(node: Any) -> None:
   307→        nonlocal session_id, started_at, cwd, branch
   308→        if isinstance(node, list):
   309→            for item in node:
   310→                visit(item)
   311→            return
   312→        if not isinstance(node, dict):
   313→            return
   314→
   315→        session_id = str(node.get("sessionId") or node.get("chatId") or node.get("id") or session_id)
   316→        started_at = earliest_timestamp(started_at, node.get("timestamp"))
   317→        cwd = str(node.get("cwd") or node.get("projectRoot") or cwd)
   318→        branch = str(node.get("branch") or branch)
   319→
   320→        role = str(node.get("role") or node.get("author") or node.get("sender") or "").lower()
   321→        timestamp = normalize_timestamp(node.get("timestamp"), started_at)
   322→        if role in {"user", "assistant", "model"}:
   323→            normalized_role = "assistant" if role == "model" else role
   324→            text = extract_gemini_text(node)
   325→            if text:
   326→                messages.append(TranscriptMessage(role=normalized_role, text=text, timestamp=timestamp))
   327→
   328→        tool_name = (
   329→            get_nested(node, "toolUse", "name")
   330→            or node.get("toolName")
   331→            or node.get("functionName")
   332→            or node.get("tool")
   333→        )
   334→        if tool_name:
   335→            tool_events.append(
   336→                TranscriptToolEvent(
   337→                    summary=f"{tool_name} input={summarize_value(node.get('args') or node.get('input'))}",
   338→                    timestamp=timestamp,
   339→                )
   340→            )
   341→
   342→        for value in node.values():
   343→            visit(value)
   344→
   345→    visit(payload)
   346→
   347→    messages = deduplicate_messages(messages)
   348→    tool_events = deduplicate_tool_events(tool_events)
   349→
   350→    return ParsedTranscript(
   351→        client="gemini",
   352→        session_id=session_id,
   353→        title=title,
   354→        started_at=started_at,
   355→        cwd=cwd,
   356→        branch=branch,
   357→        messages=messages,
   358→        tool_events=tool_events,
   359→        source_path=path,
   360→    )
   361→

   258→            slug = "myrepo"

   261→

   263→                "claude": claude_root,
   264→                "codex": Path(tmp) / ".codex",
   265→                "gemini": Path(tmp) / ".gemini",
   266→            }
   267→
   268→            # Import heartbeat modules
   269→            from _config_utils import Config, ProjectEntry  # noqa: E402
   270→            from _log_utils import LOGGER_NAME  # noqa: E402
   271→
   272→            config = Config(
   273→                projects=[ProjectEntry(path=project_root.as_posix(), name="myrepo")],
   274→                auto_push=False,
   275→            )
   276→
   277→            # Suppress logging noise
   278→            logger = logging.getLogger(LOGGER_NAME)
   279→            logger.handlers.clear()
   280→            logger.addHandler(logging.NullHandler())
   281→
   282→            from heartbeat import _process_project  # noqa: E402
   283→
   284→            with (
   285→                patch("_transcript_discover.default_client_roots", return_value=mock_roots),
   286→                patch("heartbeat.setup_logging", return_value=logger),
   287→                patch("heartbeat.get_logger", return_value=logger),
   288→                patch("heartbeat.write_alert"),
   289→                patch("heartbeat.write_alert_with_threshold"),
   290→                patch("heartbeat.reset_failure_count"),
   291→            ):
   292→                from _transcript_discover import discover_source_files as _discover  # noqa: E402
   293→                from _transcript_import import import_transcript as _import  # noqa: E402
   294→                from _transcript_parse import parse_transcript as _parse  # noqa: E402
   295→                from _transcript_discover import transcript_matches_repo as _matches  # noqa: E402
   296→                from _transcript_import import transcript_has_content as _has_content  # noqa: E402
   297→
   298→                discovered = _discover()
   299→                imported = 0
   300→                for client, source in discovered:

   302→                        parsed = _parse(client, source)
   303→                    except Exception:
   304→                        continue

   306→                        continue
   307→                    if not _matches(parsed, project_root, slug):
   308→                        continue

   311→                        root=project_root,
   312→                        global_root=global_root,
   313→                        project_slug=slug,

   315→                        mirror_to_repo=True,
   316→                    )

   318→
   319→            self.assertGreater(imported, 0, "Should have imported at least 1 transcript")

   329→                cwd=project_root, capture_output=True, text=True, check=True,
   330→            )
   331→            if status.stdout.strip():
   332→                result = subprocess.run(
   333→                    ["git", "commit", "-m", f"memorytree(transcripts): import {imported} transcript(s)"],
   334→                    cwd=project_root, capture_output=True, text=True, check=True,
   335→                )
   336→                self.assertEqual(result.returncode, 0)

1→# memorytree-workflow Skill 开发待办
     2→
     3→## 背景
     4→
     5→本仓库是 MemoryTree 记忆系统的 Skill 实现，从 `beyondchenlin/memorytree` 独立拆出。
     6→消费端项目（普通项目）通过安装此 Skill 获得记忆管理能力。
     7→
     8→## 当前核心问题
     9→
    10→大模型不可靠 — 会忘记执行 chat_log 记录、transcript 导入等机械性流程。
    11→需要把这些确定性工作交给后台进程，大模型只做轻量的摘要和状态更新。
    12→
    13→## 架构决策
    14→
    15→### 定时心跳（单次执行 + OS 调度，零 token 消耗）
    16→- 全局单实例: 1 台电脑 = 1 个定时任务，扫描所有项目
    17→- 定时扫描客户端 transcript 目录（~/.claude/projects/、~/.codex/sessions/、~/.gemini/）
    18→- 每次执行: 扫描 → 增量导入 → 清洗 → git commit + push → 退出
    19→- 心跳间隔可配置（默认 5 分钟）
    20→- 运行方式: OS 原生定时任务（cron / launchd / Task Scheduler），tmux 仅用于开发调试
    21→- Git 策略: **默认 auto_push = true**（记忆数据安全优先，防止本地丢失）
    22→
    23→### 大模型（对话时才介入，省 token）
    24→- 只写当轮 chat_log 摘要（几行文字）
    25→- 只更新 goal/todo 状态
    26→- 不负责 transcript 导入、清洗、提交
    27→
    28→---
    29→
    30→## 待办任务（按优先级排序）
    31→
    32→### P0: 定时心跳 — 核心阻塞项
    33→
    34→> 验收标准: 全局单实例 heartbeat，OS 定时任务驱动，自动发现新 transcript 并完成导入 + commit + push，无需人工介入。
    35→
    36→- [ ] **运行架构**: 单次执行 + OS 原生调度
    37→  - 核心脚本 `heartbeat.py`: 跑一次扫描就退出（无状态、幂等）
    38→  - OS 定时任务每 5 分钟调用一次
    39→  - `memorytree-daemon install`: 自动检测 OS，注册定时任务
    40→  - `memorytree-daemon run-once`: 手动执行一次（调试用）
    41→  - `memorytree-daemon watch`: tmux 循环模式（开发调试用）
    42→  - `memorytree-daemon uninstall`: 移除定时任务
    43→- [ ] **首次安装触发**: Skill 激活时若 daemon 未注册，交互式询问用户配置偏好（间隔、auto_push、范围），确认后执行 install。询问方式必须兼容所有支持 Skill 的大模型（Claude Code、Codex、Gemini CLI），不依赖特定客户端的 UI 组件

    45→- [ ] **增量导入**: 发现新 transcript 时调用 `import-transcripts.py`
    46→- [ ] **敏感信息预检**: 清洗阶段扫描常见敏感模式（API key、password、token），发现时标记警告写入日志（不自动删除，避免误伤）
    47→- [ ] **自动 git 提交 + 推送**:
    48→  - `git status --porcelain Memory/` → 无变动则跳过
    49→  - 有变动 → `git add Memory/` → `git commit` → `git push`
    50→  - **默认 auto_push = true**（记忆是用户资产，本地丢失不可恢复）
    51→  - 首次安装时提示用户确认 push 行为，之后静默执行
    52→  - 提交到当前分支（遵循项目已有的分支策略，不自动创建新分支）
    53→- [ ] **git remote 前置检查**:
    54→  - push 前检测 remote 是否存在
    55→  - 无 remote → 跳过 push，记录到日志，下次 Skill 激活时提醒用户配置
    56→- [ ] **配置文件** (`~/.memorytree/config.toml`，全局唯一):
    57→  - 心跳间隔（默认 300s）
    58→  - 监听目录列表（默认三个客户端目录）
    59→  - 已注册项目列表（自动发现或手动添加）
    60→  - auto_push 开关（默认 true）
    61→  - log_level（默认 info）

    63→  - 日志输出到 `~/.memorytree/logs/heartbeat.log`（按日轮转）
    64→  - 锁文件互斥（防止上一次还没跑完，下一次又启动）
    65→  - push 失败时记录到日志，下次重试（网络中断不丢数据）

    73→

    75→
    76→**场景**: 用户在会话 A 中讨论了很长时间但问题未解决，关闭后开新会话 B，不想重新描述所有背景。

    87→  - 按 timestamp 降序排列
    88→  - 排除当前会话自身（基于 Skill 激活时间戳：`started_at` >= 激活时间的 transcript 视为当前会话，跨客户端通用）
    89→- [ ] **延续摘要生成**（消耗 model token，但价值远大于用户手动重述）:
    90→  - 读取定位到的 transcript（优先 clean，精确确认查 raw）
    91→  - 结合 `Memory/03_chat_logs/` 已有的会话日志补充上下文

     6→# MemoryTree
     7→
     8→Use this skill for repo-level project memory. Do not treat it as an application runtime feature unless the user explicitly asks to productize it.
     9→
    10→## On Activation
    11→
    12→When this skill is invoked, immediately perform these steps without waiting for further user input:
    13→

    17→4. If `partial`: run `scripts/upgrade-memorytree.py` to add missing pieces, then report what was added.

    25→2. If MemoryTree is missing, initialize it with `scripts/init-memorytree.py`. If the script cannot run, create the files from `assets/templates/`.
    26→3. If MemoryTree is partial, upgrade it with `scripts/upgrade-memorytree.py` before manual maintenance.
    27→4. If MemoryTree is already installed, maintain only the active goal, bound todo, and current chat log. Use `references/update-rules.md`.
    28→5. Keep the installation compatible with the host repo's branch, PR, CI, and review rules. Use `references/git-policy.md`.
    29→6. MemoryTree-only git automation is allowed only inside the isolated flow in `references/git-policy.md`.
    30→7. When locale is not explicit, choose it from repo language first, then system language. Use `references/locale-selection.md`.
    31→8. Keep reply language aligned with user language first, then repo locale. Use `references/response-language.md`.
    32→9. For partial repos, use the non-destructive upgrade path before manual maintenance. Use `references/upgrade-path.md`.
    33→10. When transcript archival is enabled, import transcripts with deterministic code, preserve raw transcripts as evidence in both the current repo mirror and the global archive, generate cleaned Markdown for indexing, keep cross-project backfills and ambiguous ownership cases in the global archive only, and ask once per repository whether raw transcript files may be committed or pushed. Use `references/transcript-archive.md`.
    34→11. When scripts are needed, prefer an existing `uv run python` environment first, then a system `python`, and only fall back to manual scaffolding or conservative manual review if no runner is available. Use `references/execution-environment.md`.
    35→12. Transcript discovery, import, cleaning, and push are handled by the background heartbeat process. The model only writes chat log summaries and updates goals and todos. See `references/heartbeat-scheduling.md`.

    52→2. Classify the repo as `not-installed`, `partial`, or `installed`.
    53→3. If the repo already has stronger rules than the generated templates, preserve the repo rules and only add missing MemoryTree pieces.
    54→
    55→## Upgrade
    56→
    57→1. Use `scripts/upgrade-memorytree.py` for repositories that already have `AGENTS.md`, custom policy files, or partial `Memory/` content.
    58→2. Preserve existing repo policy files by default.
    59→3. Create only the missing MemoryTree pieces.
    60→4. Read the upgrade result and treat `agents_merge_required=true` as a manual review task, not an overwrite instruction.
    61→5. If no Python runner is available, do not create a project-local environment automatically. Fall back to conservative manual inspection and only make low-risk changes unless the user explicitly approved environment setup.
    62→
    63→## Initialize
    64→
    65→1. Run `scripts/init-memorytree.py --root <repo>` and pass `--project-name`, `--goal-summary`, and `--locale` when the user already provided them.
    66→2. Use fresh init only when the repo does not already have `AGENTS.md` or another repo policy source such as a policy-bearing `CONTRIBUTING.md`, PR templates, `CODEOWNERS`, or commitlint config. If repo policy already exists, switch to `scripts/upgrade-memorytree.py` instead of trying to skip `AGENTS.md`.
    67→3. Review the generated `AGENTS.md` before keeping it. Merge it with the repo's existing policy if needed.
    68→4. Keep the initial installation minimal: `Memory/01_goals`, `02_todos`, `03_chat_logs`, optional `04_knowledge`, `05_archive`, and `06_transcripts` only when transcript archival is enabled for the repo or needed for transcript import.
    69→5. Use the locale-specific template files in `assets/templates/<locale>/` as the source of truth for first-run scaffolding.
    70→6. Prefer `--locale auto` when the user did not request a language explicitly.
    71→7. Use `scripts/detect-memorytree-locale.py` when you need a deterministic locale check without scaffolding files.
    72→8. Prefer `uv run python` first, then a system `python`. If neither is available, create first-run files directly from `assets/templates/` instead of creating a project-local virtual environment by default.
    73→9. If transcript archival is enabled for the repo, use `scripts/import-transcripts.py` for one explicit source file and `scripts/discover-transcripts.py` when scanning local client stores. Matching transcripts must update both the repo mirror and the global archive, while unrelated projects, ambiguous ownership cases, or mismatched explicit sources are archived in the global archive only. Let the scripts generate cleaned transcripts deterministically without spending model tokens on the cleaning step.
    74→10. Ask once whether raw transcript files may also be committed to the repository. Record the answer in `AGENTS.md`, keep the files in the repo either way, and exclude `raw` files from automatic staging until the user says yes.
    75→
    76→## Maintain
    77→
    78→1. Change the active goal only after explicit user confirmation of a scope or requirement change.
    79→2. Update the active todo when progress changes, milestones move, or the next task becomes clearer.
    80→3. Append chat logs only. Never rewrite or delete prior entries.
    81→4. Keep active files small. Move stale context to archive or knowledge files instead of bloating the active goal or todo.
    82→5. Treat product ideas, architecture decisions, and operating constraints as goal or knowledge content. Treat step-by-step execution state as todo content.
    83→6. Treat cleaned transcript indexes as discovery aids, not as the final source of truth. When exact wording matters, confirm against the raw transcript archive.
    84→7. Prefer deterministic script-based transcript cleaning over manual rewriting. Do not spend model tokens to restate or normalize transcript content when `scripts/import-transcripts.py` can do it.
    85→8. Reply in the user's language when clear; otherwise align with repo locale without rewriting existing files just to translate them.
    86→
    87→## Git And Safety
    88→
    89→1. Never assume MemoryTree can override the repo's branch model.
    90→2. Default to isolated MemoryTree-only Git operations: stage only MemoryTree-owned files, use a MemoryTree-scoped commit title, push to a dedicated branch, and open a dedicated PR.
    91→3. Enable auto-merge only for MemoryTree-only PRs, and only when the repository still enforces its required review and CI checks.
    92→4. Keep repo-local raw transcript mirrors and the global transcript archive synchronized on every import. The global index must remain safe for concurrent multi-project updates.
    93→5. Keep the repository mirror limited to transcripts that belong to the current repository. Unrelated or ambiguous transcripts belong in the global archive only.
    94→6. Keep raw transcript files under `Memory/06_transcripts/raw/**` in the repo, but exclude them from automatic staging until the user explicitly approved raw transcript uploads for that repository.
    95→7. If the diff mixes product code, shared policy files, cross-project transcript archives, or unclear ownership, stop and ask the user before committing or pushing.
    96→8. If the repo has protected branches or PR-only rules, follow them even if older MemoryTree rules say otherwise.
    97→9. When `auto_push` is enabled, the heartbeat process pushes automatically after committing. If no Git remote is configured, the push is skipped. If a push fails, the heartbeat retries once. In either case an alert is written to `~/.memorytree/alerts.json`. See `references/git-policy.md`.
    98→10. During transcript cleaning, the heartbeat scans for sensitive information (API keys, passwords, tokens). Matches are logged as warnings only — no automatic deletion or redaction. See `references/heartbeat-scheduling.md`.
    99→
   100→## Resources
   101→
   102→- `references/project-detection.md`: detect install state and choose init vs maintain.
   103→- `references/memory-layout.md`: folder and file naming rules.
   104→- `references/update-rules.md`: when to version goals, todos, and session logs.
   105→- `references/git-policy.md`: safe Git defaults and policy merge guidance.
   106→- `references/locale-selection.md`: locale choice rules and alias behavior.
   107→- `references/response-language.md`: reply-language precedence and translation safety.
   108→- `references/transcript-archive.md`: raw transcript archival, clean transcript indexing, per-client source rules, and repo upload confirmation rules.
   109→- `references/upgrade-path.md`: safe adoption flow for partial repos.
   110→- `references/execution-environment.md`: how to run MemoryTree scripts without assuming a project-local Python environment.
   111→- `references/heartbeat-scheduling.md`: background heartbeat architecture, daemon CLI, and execution flow.
   112→- `references/global-configuration.md`: `~/.memorytree/` directory layout, `config.toml` schema, and `alerts.json` format.
   113→- `assets/templates/en/` and `assets/templates/zh-cn/`: seed files for English and Simplified Chinese initialization.
   114→- `scripts/heartbeat.py`: background heartbeat entry point.
   115→- `scripts/memorytree_daemon.py`: heartbeat lifecycle manager (install/uninstall/run-once/watch/status).
   116→- `scripts/recall-session.py`: on-demand transcript sync and latest session recall for cross-session context recovery.
   117→- `scripts/detect-memorytree-locale.py`: print the effective locale for a target repository.
   118→- `scripts/discover-transcripts.py`: scan supported local client stores, mirror current-project transcripts into the repo, and backfill other projects into the global archive only.
   119→- `scripts/import-transcripts.py`: import one transcript into the repo mirror and global archive, then generate clean Markdown deterministically by code.
   120→- `scripts/upgrade-memorytree.py`: safely add missing MemoryTree pieces to a partial repository.
   121→- `scripts/init-memorytree.py`: deterministic scaffold script.

   178→def _install_cron(heartbeat_script: Path, seconds: int) -> int:
   179→    if _is_cron_registered():
   180→        print("Heartbeat is already registered in cron. Use 'uninstall' first.", file=sys.stderr)
   181→        return 1
   182→
   183→    python = _python_path()
   184→    minutes = max(1, seconds // 60)
   185→    log_dir = Path.home() / ".memorytree" / "logs"
   186→    log_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
   187→
   188→    python_cmd = " ".join(shlex.quote(p) for p in python)
   189→    cron_line = (
   190→        f"*/{minutes} * * * * "
   191→        f"cd {shlex.quote(str(heartbeat_script.parent))} && "
   192→        f"{python_cmd} {shlex.quote(str(heartbeat_script))} "
   193→        f">> {shlex.quote(str(log_dir / 'heartbeat-cron.log'))} 2>&1 "
   194→        f"# memorytree"
   195→    )
   196→
   197→    existing = _get_crontab()
   198→    new_crontab = existing.rstrip("\n") + "\n" + cron_line + "\n" if existing.strip() else cron_line + "\n"
   199→
   200→    result = subprocess.run(["crontab", "-"], input=new_crontab, text=True, capture_output=True)
   201→    if result.returncode != 0:
   202→        print(f"Failed to install cron job: {result.stderr}", file=sys.stderr)
   203→        return 1
   204→
   205→    print(f"Heartbeat registered in cron (every {minutes}m).")
   206→    return 0
   207→
   208→
   209→def _uninstall_cron() -> int:
   210→    existing = _get_crontab()
   211→    filtered = "\n".join(line for line in existing.splitlines() if "memorytree" not in line)
   212→    subprocess.run(["crontab", "-"], input=filtered + "\n", text=True, capture_output=True)
   213→    print("Heartbeat removed from cron.")
   214→    return 0
   215→
   216→
   217→def _is_cron_registered() -> bool:
   218→    return "memorytree" in _get_crontab()
   219→
   220→
   221→def _get_crontab() -> str:
   222→    result = subprocess.run(["crontab", "-l"], capture_output=True, text=True)
   223→    return result.stdout if result.returncode == 0 else ""
   224→

   231→
   232→
   233→def _install_launchd(heartbeat_script: Path, seconds: int) -> int:
   234→    plist_path = _launchd_plist_path()
   235→    if plist_path.exists():
   236→        print("Heartbeat plist already exists. Use 'uninstall' first.", file=sys.stderr)
   237→        return 1
   238→
   239→    python = _python_path()
   240→    log_dir = Path.home() / ".memorytree" / "logs"
   241→    log_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
   242→
   243→    program_args = "\n".join(f"        <string>{p}</string>" for p in [*python, str(heartbeat_script)])
   244→
   245→    plist_content = f"""<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
   246→<!DOCTYPE plist PUBLIC "-//Apple//DTD PLIST 1.0//EN" "http://www.apple.com/DTDs/PropertyList-1.0.dtd">
   247→<plist version="1.0">
   248→<dict>
   249→    <key>Label</key>
   250→    <string>{LAUNCHD_LABEL}</string>
   251→    <key>ProgramArguments</key>
   252→    <array>
   253→{program_args}
   254→    </array>
   255→    <key>StartInterval</key>
   256→    <integer>{seconds}</integer>
   257→    <key>WorkingDirectory</key>
   258→    <string>{heartbeat_script.parent}</string>
   259→    <key>StandardOutPath</key>
   260→    <string>{log_dir}/heartbeat-launchd.log</string>
   261→    <key>StandardErrorPath</key>
   262→    <string>{log_dir}/heartbeat-launchd.log</string>
   263→</dict>
   264→</plist>
   265→"""
   266→    plist_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
   267→    plist_path.write_text(plist_content, encoding="utf-8")
   268→
   269→    result = subprocess.run(["launchctl", "load", str(plist_path)], capture_output=True, text=True)
   270→    if result.returncode != 0:
   271→        print(f"Failed to load plist: {result.stderr}", file=sys.stderr)
   272→        return 1
   273→
   274→    print(f"Heartbeat registered via launchd (every {seconds}s).")
   275→    return 0
   276→
   277→
   278→def _uninstall_launchd() -> int:
   279→    plist_path = _launchd_plist_path()
   280→    if plist_path.exists():
   281→        subprocess.run(["launchctl", "unload", str(plist_path)], capture_output=True)
   282→        plist_path.unlink(missing_ok=True)
   283→    print("Heartbeat removed from launchd.")
   284→    return 0
   285→
   286→
   287→def _is_launchd_registered() -> bool:
   288→    return _launchd_plist_path().exists()
   289→
   290→
   291→# ── Windows (Task Scheduler) ────────────────────────────────────────────────
   292→
   293→
   294→def _install_schtasks(heartbeat_script: Path, seconds: int) -> int:
   295→    if _is_schtasks_registered():
   296→        print("Heartbeat is already registered in Task Scheduler. Use 'uninstall' first.", file=sys.stderr)
   297→        return 1
   298→
   299→    python = _python_path()
   300→    minutes = max(1, seconds // 60)
   301→
   302→    tr_command = " ".join(f'"{p}"' for p in [*python, str(heartbeat_script)])
   303→
   304→    result = subprocess.run(
   305→        [
   306→            "schtasks", "/create",
   307→            "/tn", TASK_NAME,
   308→            "/sc", "minute",
   309→            "/mo", str(minutes),
   310→            "/tr", tr_command,
   311→            "/f",
   312→        ],
   313→        capture_output=True,
   314→        text=True,
   315→    )
   316→    if result.returncode != 0:
   317→        print(f"Failed to create scheduled task: {result.stderr}", file=sys.stderr)
   318→        return 1
   319→
   320→    print(f"Heartbeat registered in Task Scheduler (every {minutes}m).")
   321→    return 0
   322→
   323→
   324→def _uninstall_schtasks() -> int:
   325→    subprocess.run(
   326→        ["schtasks", "/delete", "/tn", TASK_NAME, "/f"],
   327→        capture_output=True,
   328→        text=True,
   329→    )
   330→    print("Heartbeat removed from Task Scheduler.")
   331→    return 0
   332→
   333→
   334→def _is_schtasks_registered() -> bool:
   335→    result = subprocess.run(
   336→        ["schtasks", "/query", "/tn", TASK_NAME],
   337→        capture_output=True,
   338→        text=True,
   339→    )
   340→    return result.returncode == 0
   341→
   342→
   343→# ── Helpers ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   344→
   345→
   346→def _heartbeat_script_path() -> Path:
   347→    return Path(__file__).resolve().parent / "heartbeat.py"
   348→
   349→
   350→def _python_path() -> list[str]:
   351→    uv = shutil.which("uv")
   352→    if uv:
   353→        return [uv, "run", "python"]
   354→    return [sys.executable]
   355→

   357→if __name__ == "__main__":
   358→    sys.exit(main())
